# Paradiso - Canto 11

### 1 O insensata cura de’ mortali,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: O senseless eagerness of mortals,
- **gemini1-ja**: ああ、愚かな人々の執着よ、
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>O</td><td>insensata</td><td>cura</td><td>de’</td><td>mortali</td></tr>
<tr><th>Lemma</th><td>o</td><td>insensato</td><td>cura</td><td>di + i</td><td>mortale</td></tr>
<tr><th>Part of Speech</th><td>interjection</td><td>adjective</td><td>noun</td><td>preposition</td><td>noun</td></tr>
<tr><th>Gender</th><td></td><td>f.</td><td>f.</td><td>m.</td><td>m.</td></tr>
<tr><th>Number</th><td></td><td>sg.</td><td>sg.</td><td>pl.</td><td>pl.</td></tr>

<tr><th>Latin</th><td>O</td><td>insensatus</td><td>cura</td><td>de + i</td><td>mortalis</td></tr>
<tr><th>Interlingua</th><td>O</td><td>insensate</td><td>cura</td><td>de + le</td><td>mortal</td></tr>
<tr><th>French</th><td>O</td><td>insensé</td><td>soin</td><td>des</td><td>mortels</td></tr>
<tr><th>Spanish</th><td>O</td><td>insensato</td><td>cuidado</td><td>de los</td><td>mortales</td></tr>
<tr><th>Portuguese</th><td>O</td><td>insensato</td><td>cuidado</td><td>dos</td><td>mortais</td></tr>
<tr><th>Romanian</th><td>O</td><td>nesentema</td><td>grijă</td><td>al</td><td>muritori</td></tr>
<tr><th>Esperanto</th><td>O</td><td>sensenta</td><td>zorgo</td><td>de laj</td><td>mortaloj</td></tr>
<tr><th>Derived</th><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td></tr>

</table>

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: O senseless care of mortals,
- **gemma3-ja**: ああ、死者の無思慮な心配よ、

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: O senseless cure of mortals,  
- **gptoss-ja**: おお、愚かな人間の治療よ、

### 2 quanto son difettivi silogismi

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: how defective are the syllogisms
- **gemini1-ja**: どれほど不完全な推論なのか、

### 3 quei che ti fanno in basso batter l’ali!

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: that make you beat your wings downward!
- **gemini1-ja**: お前を地に這わせるものは！
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>quei</td><td>che</td><td>ti</td><td>fanno</td><td>in</td><td>basso</td><td>batter</td><td>l’</td><td>ali</td></tr>

<tr><th>Latin</th><td>ille</td><td>quod</td><td>tu</td><td>facere</td><td>in</td><td>bassus</td><td>battuere</td><td>ille</td><td>ala</td></tr>

- **gemma3-en**: those that make you beat your wings low!
- **gemma3-ja**: それらはあなたに翼を低く羽ばたかせるのか！

### 9 s’affaticava e chi si dava a l’ozio,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and another gave himself up to idleness,
- **gemini1-ja**: 苦労する者もいれば、怠惰にふける者もいる

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: labored and who gave himself to idleness,
- **gemma3-ja**: 疲弊する者もいれば、怠惰に身を委ねる者もいる。

### 27 e qui è uopo che ben si distingua.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and here it is necessary to make a fine distinction.

- **gemini1-ja**: この斜面で、その急峻さが最も崩れる場所で、

### 50 più sua rattezza, nacque al mondo un sole,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: its steepness most, a sun was born into the world,
- **gemini1-ja**: 太陽が生まれた。

### 51 come fa questo talvolta di Gange.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: as this one sometimes does from the Ganges.
- **gemini1-ja**: ガンジス川で時々起こることと同じように。

### 52 Però chi d’esso loco fa parole,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Therefore, whoever speaks of that place,
- **gemini1-ja**: だからその場所について語る者は、

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Therefore whoever of that place makes words,
- **gemma3-ja**: だから、その場所について言葉を述べる者は、

### 53 non dica Ascesi, ché direbbe corto,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: should not say Assisi, for that would be too short,
- **gemini1-ja**: アッシジとは言わず、それは不十分だからだ。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: let him not say Ascesi, because he would say little,
- **gemma3-ja**: アシェージとは言わないように、それは短すぎるだろう、

### 54 ma Orïente, se proprio dir vuole.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: but Orient, if he wants to say it properly.
- **gemini1-ja**: 正確に言いたいなら、オリエンテと言わなければならない。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: but Orient, if he truly wants to say it.
- **gemma3-ja**: しかし、もし正確に言いたいのであれば、オリエンテ（東）と言うべきだ。

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: but Orïente, if truly to say wants.
- **gptoss-ja**: ただし Orïente、もし本当に言いたいのであれば。

### 62 et coram patre le si fece unito;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and coram patre he united himself to her;
- **gemini1-ja**: そして父の前で、彼は彼女と結ばれた。

### 80 si scalzò prima, e dietro a tanta pace

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: was the first to take off his shoes, and he ran after such peace
- **gemini1-ja**: まず靴を脱ぎ、その大きな平和の後を

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: took off his shoes first, and behind such peace
- **gemma3-ja**: まず靴を脱ぎ、そしてそのような平和の後ろに

### 81 corse e, correndo, li parve esser tardo.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and, as he ran, it seemed to him that he was slow.
- **gemini1-ja**: 走り、走りながら、遅れているように思えた

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: ran and, running, it seemed to him to be slow.
- **gemma3-ja**: 走り、走っている間、遅れているように感じた。

### 108 che le sue membra due anni portarno.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: which his body bore for two years.
- **gemini1-ja**: 彼の体は2年間それを身に着けていた

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: which his limbs carried for two years.
- **gemma3-ja**: その彼の肢体は2年間運んだ。
